				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h3 style="text-align: center;">Hi! We&#8217;re the Willard&#8217;s</h3>
<p>We spent two years full-time RVing and boondocked the majority of the time. Now we&#8217;ve transitioned to part-time RV life.</p>
<p>During the planning and the &#8220;adventure&#8221; phases, we gained much knowledge and experience.</p>
<p>We hope to share our story with you so that you can consider living an extraordinary life!</p>

<p style="text-align: center;"><strong></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><strong>Not sure what you need (and don&#8217;t need)?  </strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">There&#8217;s a lot of &#8220;stuff&#8221; on the market that you really don&#8217;t need in an RV. But there&#8217;s also some essential gear.</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://resetyourjourney.com//gear/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Here&#8217;s</a> a list of some of that gear you&#8217;ll need living or vacationing in an RV or travel trailer. As well as some of the things that are nice to have along the journey. But none of the stuff you don&#8217;t need!</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">We use affiliate links for the gear we suggest, but if it&#8217;s not useful or well made, it never made the cut.</p>
